<Date>1530376663338</Date><Rating>5< /Rating>< text>
This is seriously the most friendly dentistry office I've EVER been to! The people at the front desk are always pleasant and remember their clients and are extremely helpful, the dental hygienists are friendly and gentle on those gums, and the dentist is very good at his job! I was so impressed with this place that not only am I a lifelong client, but so is my husband and elderly father!

Their prices are a bit high but comparative to most other dentist offices, and if you have dental insurance they are very good about making sure things go through your insurance first before they do anything.

My father ended up getting a full extraction and a full set of dentures from here and while the price was high (it is anywhere!) they were VERY helpful and compassionate through the whole process. They even would give him phone calls to check up on him and see how he's adjusting!

The ONLY downside to this place is their office is a bit hard to find (which isn't their fault, its how the building is set up) and their waiting room is small. They do the best they can with the small space they have though. Seriously, if you are looking for a new dentist go here!!</text>

<text>Found Shear Vanity on Yelp. Made an appointment on Sunday despite the salon being closed on sunday and monday I got a response when I emailed them. I got a call from Esther on the day I wanted to go in and told I'd be good to come in.
I went in for a cut. I went from mid back length hair to just above my shoulders and I love it!!!
Jessica shampooed and conditioned before doing most of the cut and Esther gave it some texture before Jessica finished with the style I had asked for. She knew what to do to get my curly hair to cooperate and it came out great!
The salon is a pretty big size and it's open, clean, and welcoming as was the receptionist at the front.
I felt pampered and I liked the vibe!!
I'm definitely going to go back as I would like to maintain this short length for a while and I'll definitely need to get it trimmed from time to time.

< review>
My wedding was in March and I didn't know where to get my hair and makeup done so I was really stressed. A coworker recommended this establishment, I was a bit skeptical at first since I only saw one picture of my friend when she got her makeup done. I also saw some of their instagram pictures. I didn't have an idea of how I wanted my hair and as for my makeup I didn't want to look like someone totally different. The day of, I got to my appointment and they were very nice and welcoming offered refreshments i.e coffee or water. The staff was very attentive and it was a busy Saturday morning. I absolutely LOVED the updo and the makeup. Very elegant and vintage, just exactly what I imagined. I got many compliments from my guests and family. I would definitely refer my friends and family here. To top it all off I wasn't overcharged like other places. I was an extremely satisfied customer. Thank you Sheer Vanity staff for the time and dedication you take to enhance the beauty of women.< /review>

< Review>
Best food ever. It's location is the original hat. Prices are great for the food. I believe there are 9 locations & out of all the locations. I've been to 7 out of 9.

The ones I've been to we're the best. I've tried almost all of the choices. And have not been disappointed yet.

Be certain when ordering fries and onion rings. Order a small one.
Because a small one is for two and a large is for at least 4 to 5 people.

It's certain that you'll have to go back more than once to try out all the food. Because you're not going to be able to try them all out in one day.
Enjoy.<//Review>

<Review>Pastrami-centric joint serving up some great pastrami fries. They're currently operating during coronavirus both through drive through and for takeout. I would suggest calling ahead to place your order as the drive through line was long. They had our food ready in ~15 min. There was a minor issue when we called in the order; the first time, the person on the other side didn't hear us and the second time the call didn't go through. Third times a charm though, so luckily we were able to indulge.

This isn't on the menu, but if you want to have a lunch that serves 3-4 people, you can order the wet fries (the gravy it comes with is so creamy and heavy) with pastrami and cheese on top (extra for both items). The pastrami is thinly sliced and they do not skimp. They did a good job of mixing the things so that even the fries on the bottom had a mix of gravy and pastrami in there. The fries are standard cut and we're piping hot. We went into a minor food coma afterwards

It's super clean inside. They do take credit cards. Service is quick and efficient. Overall it's a good spot to partake in pastrami and treat yourself should you ever find yourself around the Brea Mall.< /Review>< Pictures>

< Text>
I can't remember a time when The Hat wasn't a local favorite.

The food is excellent. All of it. Personally, the best is their chili-cheese fries.

I'm not exaggerating when I say I gained at LEAST 15 lbs in my mid 20's eating WAAAAAY too much chili-cheese fries with pastrami.

The Hat's Pastrami are the standard for all other Pastrami places.

Parking's just okay. Traffic in the area is terrible. But the food is worth it. It's been around for almost 70 years for a reason.<//Text>

< name>
Janet Birrueta J.D.< /name>
< Time>
1567638618067<//Time>
<rate>3<//rate>< Review>
SERVICE:  I was the only customer and the person who took my order (an older man who appeared to be the manager) was not friendly at all.  However, the food was served fast and the young man who handed me my food was friendly.
PRICES:  I ordered a regular pastrami sandwich (their specialty), small fries and a medium drink.  I paid $18.36 - WOW.  I found this to be overpriced for a sandwich meal at an old walk-up fast food joint (with no indoor seating) in Alhambra.
FOOD:  The food was served hot and freshly prepared.  The sandwich was standard in size (on a standard roll), but overflowing in pastrami.  It was A LOT of pastrami. The pastrami itself was good and juicy, but nothing special.  The small/medium fries were actually extra large fries (I was given a paper lunch bag half full of fries).  The fries were thick and good, but also A LOT.  The drink (horchata) was too sugary.  I had to water down the horchata to drink it.
SUMMARY: This is an OKAY place for pastrami, but definitely not a place I would crave or make an effort to return to, especially not at those prices.</Review>

<rating>3< /rating>< review>
I have been here several times. The prices seem quite high given that you're essentially ordering a sandwich. I paid about $25 for two sandwiches and fries. But when you open the sandwiches, you'll find a GENEROUS portion. I ordered two pastrami dip sandwiches. And they did NOT skimp on the pastrami! So much pastrami!

The sandwich was pretty salty, however. And the fries portion was enormous! I ordered a small and it looked like they gave me enough for a party of 6. I really tried to eat as much as I could but only could eat about half of them. You definitely get what you pay for here. But I would recommend drinking tons of fluids (water, preferably) as the sodium content here is probably through the roof.<//review>

< rate>

< Review>
The food here is decent tasting good but nothing extraordinary. What IS extraordinary are the portions. WOW! I've never eaten at The Hat so I walked up and ordered like I normally do at any burger joint. I ordered a pastrami dip for me, one for my husband, a cheeseburger for each of my two kids, an order of fries, an order of onion rings for my husband and chili cheese fries for me. They don't have meal "combos" so I figured I'd make up my own. BIG mistake lol. My hubby and I were hard pressed to finish HALF of one pastrami, much less a full one. We all picked from the chili cheese fries and still had at least half to bring home with us. We each had one or two onion rings just to taste them and sampled a fry or two as well. We ended up overstuffed and still had about 2/3 of our meal left over. Like I said, the food is typical L.A. fast food, tasty but nothing life changing but come hungry and bring someone to share with because ONE item off this menu is enough to fill you up plus have tasty leftover. FYI its is a bit pricey for fast food (all this plus four large drinks set us back $62) but keep in mind that you are paying for 3 or 4 times the normal burger joint servings. It's the perfect spot to come with a group, order a couple of items and share.</Review>

<Rate>5</Rate>< text>
I have been in the SGV for almost 10 years now and up until this year, had never tried The Hat. Boy that was a mistake. I LOVE IT. The pastrami sandwiches are HUGE and brimming with yummy pickles and mustard (the only way a sandwich should be in my opinion). The most recent time that I went, I got a pastrami sandwich and chili cheese fries to share with a friend. I should have known better than to assume that this was enough food to satisfy two people. It was more like a platter for 3-4. They put the chili cheese fries on top of a 4-compartment cup holder and it has a GENEROUS scoop of chili and cheese on top of the fries. I think I took 3 bites after finishing my half of the sandwich and called it quits. I need to go back and try to tame that beast one more time but this time, I'll bring more back up! >:]</text>

Rodney S</username>

< Text>
The Hat, I tip my hat to thee!

If you need fries in caveman proportions, then look no further.  For The Hat, is where it's at!

The OG location that started it all, The Hat in Alhambra is an old school food stand, complete with walk-up windows for ordering & pick up, along with a covered patio dining area.  For my inaugural visit, I pondered whether to order their famous pastrami dip or go with their wet fries.  I've read how their servings of fries are quite generous, and being how I try not to eat bread, I thought an order of loaded wet fries was that particular day's calling.

Wet fries w/ added pastrami, tomatoes, pickles & mustard-
Holy crap!  It looks like a food challenge!  I thought the chatter about portions were simply hyperbole, like a tall tale being altered with exaggerations until the details became comical.  But, alas, I wasn't prepared for what lied before me.  I watched my order prepared right before my very eyes.  From thick fries fresh from the fryer, to the slathering of savory brown gravy, the addition of tender, juicy pastrami, to the addition of a pound of dill pickle slices & tomatoes, to the cherry on top being a delicious dollop of mustard, I saw the assemblage of this calorie-busting behemoth from birth to readiness graduation.  The customers after me marveled at the huge portions of my loaded wet fries being prepared, which, like a proud parent, I boasted "Yeah, that's mine."

After laying claim to a table, I dug into my gargantuan meal.  Each bite, wondrous & delightful.  The fries had the perfect thickness to handle the weight of all that smothered them.  The gravy salty & creamy.  The pastrami wonderfully fatty.  The amount of pickles seemed almost ridiculous.  After 5 minutes of going at it, the loaded wet fries seemed like I hardly put a dent in them.  They mocked me, saying "Is that the best you got, bub?"  I did my best to devour the most I could, knowing I'd have to take this monstrosity home to await it's final fate later on for dinner.

Besides the usual condiments, all you can grab whole chili peppers are a must if you're a heat lover.  They're a perfect compliment to the copious amounts of food at The Hat.

Service was good.  Ordering at the window was quick, and I didn't wait long for my fries to be ready.  Ample tables to dine at, with parking in a private lot.  The Hat is conveniently located minutes north of the 10 freeway at the intersection of Valley & Garfield.

Hunger need not show it's ugly head here.  The Hat serves ginormous amounts of food quickly for the famished masses.  I managed to finish my loaded wet fries after 2 meals.  This coming from a guy with a healthy appetite.  I'd imagine some might go a whole day to accomplish that.  Of course, sharing would be a good idea, but I'm not into that.  I want this baby all to myself.  My first visit here, and I see why The Hat is a beloved SGV institution.  If I'm in the area again, and I don't care about calories & BMI, then I'm definitely dropping by for another go at The Hat.

Highly recommend!
NOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOM<//Text>

<user_name>Kara patino</user_name>< date>
1464246311320</date>
<Rate>4<//Rate>< text>
So I heard from people and friends I must try this place out so I did and decided to come to this location. It reminded me so much of Tommys Burgers because its at the corner of both busy mainstreets. So the menu of this place didnt surprise me as much as I thought it would but for its price its cheap. So I decided to order the BBQ Beef Pastrami here and a side of onion rings. The moment you bit the Pastrami Beef BBQ sandwich all I tasted was the BBQ. It felt like there was no meat here :/ and the sauce its self has overwhelmed the beef by 90%. But other than that the onion rings did not dissapoint me they were worth buying it cost $4 something and were given alot in the bag. Other than that this place was a good experience next time Ill just order the regular pastrami sandwich instead.< /text>
